职责：包含任务类型、业务对象关联、重试策略、优先级等平台级元信息\n// 关系：Task → Job（一个 Task 可以产生多个 Job，用于重试）\nmodel Task {\n  id             String     @id @default(uuid())\n  organizationId String\n  projectId      String\n  type  Int        @default(3)\n  retryCount     Int        @default(0)\n  error          String?\n  workerId       String? // 实际执行该 Task 的 Worker 节点 ID\n  traceId        String? // Stage13-Final: Pipeline 级 traceId（用于 CE Core Layer 审计追溯）\n  createdAt      DateTime   @default(now())\n  updatedAt      DateTime   @updatedAt\n\n  jobs ShotJob[] @relation(\"TaskJobs\")\n\n  project      Project      @relation(\"ProjectTasks\", fields: [projectId], references: [id])\n  organization Organization @relation(\"OrganizationTasks\", fields: [organizationId], references: [id])\n  worker       WorkerNode?  @relation(\"TaskWorker\", fields: [workerId], references: [id])\n\n  @@index([status, createdAt])\n}\n\n// WorkerJob（Worker 执行记录）\n// 定义：Worker 维度的一次具体执行记录\n// 职责：记录 Worker 执行任务的过程和结果\n// 关系：WorkerJob 与 Task/Job 是不同层面的概念，WorkerJob 主要用于 Worker 内部调度和计费\nmodel WorkerJob {\n  id            String          @id @default(uuid())\n  type          WorkerJobType\n  payload       Json // { taskData, params, modelInfo }\n  status        WorkerJobStatus @default(pending)\n  workerId      String?\n  retryCount    Int             @default(0)\n  traceId       String\n  jobId         String          @unique // BullMQ jobId\n  engineVersion String?\n  modelVersion  String?\n  createdAt     DateTime        @default(now())\n  updatedAt     DateTime        @updatedAt\n\n  // Relations\n  worker        WorkerNode?    @relation(\"WorkerNodeJobs\", fields: [workerId], references: [id])\n  billingEvents BillingEvent[] @relation(\"BillingEventJob\")\n\n  @@map(\"worker_jobs\")\n}\n\n// Job（Worker 执行单元）\n// 定义：某个 Worker 在某个时间执行某个 Task 的一次尝试\n// 职责：记录单次执行的状态、结果、错误信息等\n// 关系：Job 属于某个 Task（taskId），一个 Task 可以产生多个 Job（用于重试）\n// Studio v0.2: Shot 生成任务模型\n// Studio v0.4: 增强队列化处理能力\n// Studio v0.8: 引入 Task 层，Job 关联 Task\nmodel ShotJob {\n  id             String    @id @default(uuid())\n  organizationId String\n  projectId      String\n  episodeId      String\n  sceneId        String\n  shotId         String\n  taskId         String?\n  workerId       String?\n  status         JobStatus @default(PENDING)\n  type           JobType\n  priority       Int       @default(0)\n  maxRetry       Int       @default(3)\n  retryCount     Int       @default(0)\n  attempts       Int       @default(0)\n  payload        Json?\n  engineConfig   Json?\n  lastError      String?\n  traceId        String? // Stage13: 用于 CE Core Layer 审计追溯\n  createdAt      DateTime  @default(now())\n  updatedAt      DateTime  @updatedAt\n\n  shot         Shot         @relation(\"ShotJobs\", fields: [shotId], references: [id])\n  task         Task?        @relation(\"TaskJobs\", fields: [taskId], references: [id])\n  worker       WorkerNode?  @relation(\"WorkerNodeShotJobs\", fields: [workerId], references: [id])\n  project      Project      @relation(\"ProjectShotJobs\", fields: [projectId], references: [id])\n  episode      Episode      @relation(\"EpisodeShotJobs\", fields: [episodeId], references: [id])\n  scene        Scene        @relation(\"SceneShotJobs\", fields: [sceneId], references: [id])\n  organization Organization @relation(\"OrganizationShotJobs\", fields: [organizationId], references: [id])\n}\n\nmodel WorkerNode {\n  id            String       @id @default(uuid())\n  workerId      String       @unique\n  name          String? // Worker 名称（可选）\n  status        WorkerStatus @default(offline)\n  gpuCount      Int          @default(0)\n  gpuMemory     Int          @default(0)\n  gpuType       String       @default(\"unknown\")\n  tasksRunning  Int          @default(0)\n  temperature   Float?\n  capabilities  Json         @default(\"{}\") // { supportedJobTypes[], supportedModels[], maxBatchSize }\n  lastHeartbeat DateTime     @default(now())\n  createdAt     DateTime     @default(now())\n  updatedAt     DateTime     @updatedAt\n\n  // Relations\n  jobs     WorkerJob[] @relation(\"WorkerNodeJobs\")\n  shotJobs ShotJob[]   @relation(\"WorkerNodeShotJobs\") // Orchestrator Stage2: 关联 ShotJob\n  tasks    Task[]      @relation(\"TaskWorker\") // S1-FIX-A: Task 关联 Worker\n\n  @@index([status])\n  @@map(\"worker_nodes\")\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// 模型宇宙体系 (Model Universe System)\n// ============================================\n\nmodel ModelRegistry {\n  id                 String    @id @default(uuid())\n  name               String\n  type               ModelType\n  version            String\n  changelog          String?\n  compatibleEngines  Json // { engines: @default(now())\n  updatedAt          DateTime  @updatedAt\n\n  @@unique([name, version])\n  @@map(\"model_registry\")\n}\n\nmodel TemplatePreset {\n  id        String       @id @default(uuid())\n @@map(\"template_presets\")\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// 质量与安全体系 (Quality & Safety System)\n// ============================================\n\nmodel QualityScore {\n  id 商业化体系 (Billing System)\n// ============================================\n\nmodel BillingEvent {\n  id                 String           @id @default(uuid())\n  eventType          BillingEventType\n // Relations\n  project      Project            @relation(\"ProjectNovelSources\", fields: [projectId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)\n  analysisJobs NovelAnalysisJob[] @relation(\"NovelSourceAnalysisJobs\")\n  chapters     NovelChapter[]     @relation(\"NovelSourceChapters\")\n\n  @@index([projectId])\n  @@map(\"novel_sources\")\n}\n\nmodel NovelChapter {\n  id             String   @id @default(uuid())\n  novelSourceId  String\n  orderIndex     Int // 章节顺序（从1开始）\n  title          String // 章节标题\n  rawText        String   @db.Text // 章节原始文本（UTF-8）\n  summary        String?  @db.Text // S1-FIX-A: 引擎对章节的摘要，后续由小说分析引擎生成\n  startParagraph Int? // 起始段落索引（在原始文本中的位置）\n  endParagraph   Int? // 结束段落索引\n  characterCount Int? // 章节字符数\n  createdAt      DateTime @@map(\"novel_analysis_status\")\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// API Key 安全体系 (API Key Security System)\n// ============================================\n\n// API Key 模型（用于机器/Worker/外部服务认证）\n// 支持 HMAC + Nonce + Timestamp 签名机制\nmodel ApiKey {\n  id          String       @id @default(uuid())\n  key         String       @unique // 公钥 ID（对外暴露，例如：ak_xxx）\n  secretHash  String // 密钥哈希（使用 bcrypt 或类似算法，不存明文）\n  name        String? // 可选的 API Key 名称（便于管理）\n  ownerUserId String? // 可选，关联用户\n  ownerOrgId  String? // 可选，关联组织\n  status      ApiKeyStatus @default(ACTIVE) // 状态：ACTIVE / DISABLED\n  lastUsedAt  DateTime? // 最后使用时间\n  expiresAt   DateTime? // 过期时间（可选）\n  createdAt   DateTime     @default(now())\n  updatedAt   DateTime     @updatedAt\n\n  // Relations\n  ownerUser User?         @relation(\"UserApiKeys\", fields: [ownerUserId], references: [id])\n  ownerOrg  Organization? @relation(\"OrganizationApiKeys\", fields: [ownerOrgId], references: [id])\n  auditLogs AuditLog[]    @relation(\"ApiKeyAuditLogs\") // 审计日志关联\n\n  @@index([key])\n  @@index([status])\n  @@index([ownerUserId])\n  @@index([ownerOrgId])\n  @@map(\"api_keys\")\n}\n\nenum ApiKeyStatus {\n  ACTIVE\n  DISABLED\n\n  @@map(\"api_key_status\")\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// 审计日志体系 (Audit Log System)\n// ============================================\n\n// 审计日志模型（用于记录关键操作）\n// 支持 JWT 用户和 API Key 两种认证来源\nmodel AuditLog {\n  id           String    @id @default(uuid())\n  userId       String? // JWT 用户 ID，可为空\n  apiKeyId     String? // 对应 ApiKey.id，可为空（HMAC 调用场景）\n  action       String // 动作标识：PROJECT_CREATED / TASK_CREATED / JOB_SUCCEEDED 等\n  resourceType String // 资源类型：project / episode / scene / shot / task / job / worker / auth 等\n  resourceId   String? // 资源主键 ID，可为空\n  ip           String? // 请求 IP\n  userAgent    String?   @db.Text // UA 字符串\n  // V1.1: 记录签名相关字段\n  nonce        String?\n  signature    String?\n  timestamp    DateTime?\n  details      Json? // 附加信息（请求参数、结果摘要等）\n  payload      Json? // S1-FIX-A: 规范向 payload：包含 action/resourceType/resourceId/ip/ua/nonce/signature/timestamp/details 等的完整快照\n  createdAt    DateTime  @default(now())\n\n  // Relations\n  user   User?   @relation(\"UserAuditLogs\", fields: [userId], references: [id])\n  apiKey ApiKey? @relation(\"ApiKeyAuditLogs\", fields: [apiKeyId], references: [id])\n\n  @@index([createdAt])\n  @@index([action])\n  @@index([resourceType, resourceId])\n  @@index([userId])\n  @@index([apiKeyId])\n  @@index([nonce, timestamp])\n  @@map(\"audit_logs\")\n}\n\n// ============================================\n// Media & Security (ADD_SAFE
